A and B are guilty of \nconspiring to cheat the Government the moment that one of them drafts the \nfraudulent tender document or engages in any other act in furtherance of the \nplan. \n \n(d)  A, B and C agree to engage in fraud and misuse of visas, permits or \nother documents to facilitate a particular act of terrorism in Malaysia. All three \nare guilty of conspiracy to provide support for the commission of a terrorist act \nthe moment any one of them engages in an act in furtherance of the plan, such \nas acquiring the visas or other materials necessary to produce the fraudulent \ndocuments. \n \n \nPunishment of criminal conspiracy \n \n120B. (1) \nWhoever is a party to a criminal conspiracy to commit an \noffence punishable with death, imprisonment for a term of two years \nor upwards shall, where no express provision is made in this Code for \nthe punishment of such a conspiracy, be punished in the same manner \nas if he had abetted such offence.\n\n76                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n(2) Subject to subsection (3), whoever is a party to a criminal \nconspiracy other than a criminal conspiracy to commit an offence \npunishable as aforesaid shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nnot exceeding six months or with fine or with both. \n \n(3) If the offence, the commission of which is the object of the \nconspiracy, is a minor offence under the Minor Offences Act 1955  \n[Act 336] the punishment for such conspiracy shall not exceed the \nmaximum punishment provided for such minor offence. \n \n \nCHAPTER VI \n \nOFFENCES AGAINST THE STATE \n \nWaging or attempting to wage war or abetting the waging of war \nagainst the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, a Ruler or Yang di-Pertua \nNegeri \n \n121. Whoever wages war against the Yang di-Pertuan Agong or \nagainst any of the Rulers or Yang di-Pertua Negeri, or attempts to wage \nsuch war, or abets the waging of such war, shall be punished with death \nor imprisonment for life, and if not sentenced to death shall also be \nliable to fine. \n \n \nOffences against the person of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, Ruler \nor Yang di-Pertua Negeri \n \n121A. \nWhoever compasses, imagines, invents, devises or intends the \ndeath of or hurt to or imprisonment or restraint of the Yang di-Pertuan \nAgong or any of the Rulers or Yang di-Pertua Negeri, their heirs or \nsuccessors, shall be punished with death and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nOffences against the authority of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, \nRuler or Yang di-Pertua Negeri \n \n121B. \nWhoever compasses, imagines, invents or intends the\n\nPenal Code                                            77 \n \ndeposition or deprivation of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong from the \nsovereignty of Malaysia or the deprivation or deposition of the Ruler, \nhis heirs or successors, or of the Yang di-Pertua Negeri from the rule \nof a State, or the overawing by means of criminal force or the show of \ncriminal force the Government of Malaysia or of any State, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for life and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nAbetting offences under section 121A or 121B \n \n121C. \nWhoever abets the commission of any of the offences \npunishable by section 121A or 121B shall be punished with the \npunishment provided for the said offences. \n \n \nIntentional omission to give information of offences against section \n121, 121A, 121B or 121C by a person bound to inform \n \n121D. \nWhoever knowing or having reason to believe that any \noffence punishable under section 121, 121A, 121B or 121C has been \ncommitted intentionally omits to give any information respecting that \noffence, which he is legally bound to give, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to seven years or with fine \nor with both. \n \n \nCollecting arms, etc., with the intention of waging war against the \nYang di-Pertuan Agong, a Ruler or Yang di-Pertua Negeri \n \n122. Whoever collects or attempts to collect men, arms or \nammunition, or otherwise prepares to wage war with the intention of \neither waging or being prepared to wage war against the Yang di-\nPertuan Agong or any of the Rulers or the Yang di-Pertua Negeri or \nabets the waging or the preparation of such war, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for life or imprisonment for a term not exceeding twenty \nyears, and shall also be liable to fine.\n\n78                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nConcealing with intent to facilitate a design to wage war \n \n123. Whoever by any act, or by illegal omission, conceals or attempts \nto conceal the existence of a design to wage war against the Yang di-\nPertuan Agong or any of the Rulers or the Yang di-Pertua Negeri, \nintending by such concealment or  attempted concealment to facilitate, \nor knowing it to be likely that such concealment or attempted \nconcealment will facilitate, the waging of such war, shall be punished \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to ten years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n \nAssaulting member of Parliament, etc., with intent to compel or \nrestrain the exercise of any lawful power \n \n124. Whoever, with the intention of inducing or compelling or \nattempting to induce or compel a member of Parliament or of any \nLegislative Assembly or of any State Executive Council to exercise or \nrefrain from exercising in any manner the lawful powers of such \nmember, assaults or wrongfully restrains, or attempts wrongfully to \nrestrain, or overawes by means of criminal force, or the show of \ncriminal force, or attempts so to overawe, such member shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to seven \nyears, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \n124A. (Deleted by F.M.S. En. 13 of 1939). \n \n \nActivity detrimental to parliamentary democracy \n \n124B. Whoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, commits an \nactivity detrimental to parliamentary democracy shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to twenty years.\n\nPenal Code                                            79 \n \nAttempt to commit activity detrimental to parliamentary \ndemocracy \n \n124C. Whoever attempts to commit an activity detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy or does any act preparatory thereto shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to fifteen \nyears. \n \n \nPrinting, sale, etc., of documents and publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy \n \n124D. Whoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, prints, \npublicises, sells, issues, circulates or reproduces any document or \npublication detrimental to parliamentary democracy shall be punished \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to fifteen years: \n \nProvided that no person shall be convicted of an offence under this \nsection if he proves to the satisfaction of the court that the document \nor publication in respect of which he is charged was printed, published, \nsold, issued, circulated or reproduced, as the case may be, without his \nauthority, consent and knowledge, and without any want of due care \nor caution on his part, and that he did not know and had no reason to \nsuspect the nature of the document or publication. \n \n \nPossession of documents and publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy \n \n124E. (1) \nAny person who, without lawful excuse, has in his \npossession any document or publication detrimental to parliamentary \ndemocracy or any extract therefrom, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to ten years. \n \n(2) The document and publication referred to in subsection (1) shall \nbe presumed to be a document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy until the contrary is proved; and where in \nany prosecution under this section it is proved that a person was \ncarrying or had in his possession or under his control a document or \npublication detrimental to parliamentary democracy he shall be\n\n80                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \ndeemed to have known the contents and the nature of the contents of \nsuch document or publication: \n \nProvided that no person shall be convicted of an offence under this \nsection if he proves to the satisfaction of the court \u2014 \n \n(a) that he was not aware of the contents and the nature of the \ncontents of the document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy which he was carrying or had in \nhis possession or under his control; and \n \n(b) that he was carrying or had the document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy in his possession \nor under his control in such circumstances that at no time \ndid he have reasonable cause to believe or suspect that the \ndocument or publication was a document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy. \n \n \nImportation of document and publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy \n \n124F. (1) \nAny person who imports or attempts to import or abets \nthe importation of any document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy or without lawful excuse has in his \npossession any document or publication shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to five years. \n \n(2) The document and publication referred to in subsection (1) shall \nbe presumed to be a document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy until the contrary is proved; and where in \nany prosecution under this section it is proved that a person was \ncarrying or had in his possession or under his control a document or \npublication detrimental to parliamentary democracy he shall be \ndeemed to have known the contents and the nature of the contents of \nsuch document or publication: \n \nProvided that no person shall be convicted of an offence under this \nsection if he proves to the satisfaction of the court \u2014\n\nPenal Code                                            81 \n \n \n(a) that he was not aware of the contents and the nature of the \ncontents of the document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy which he was carrying or had in \nhis possession or under his control; and \n \n(b) that he was carrying or had the document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy in his possession \nor under his control in such circumstances that at no time \ndid he have reasonable cause to believe or suspect that the \ndocument or publication was a document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy. \n \n \nPosting of placards, etc.  \n \n124G. Any person who posts or distributes any placard, circular or \nother document containing any incitement to violence, or counselling \nviolent disobedience to the law or to any lawful order, or likely to lead \nto any breach of the peace, shall be punished with imprisonment for a \nterm which may extend to five years. \n \n \nDissemination of information \n \n124H. Any person who by word of mouth or in writing or in any \nnewspaper, periodical, book, circular, or other printed publication or \nby any other means including electronic means incites violence, or \ncounsels violent disobedience to the law or to any lawful order, shall \nbe punished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to five \nyears. \n \n \nDissemination of false reports \n \n124I. Any person who, by word of mouth or in writing or in any \nnewspaper, periodical, book, circular, or other printed publication or \nby any other means including electronic means spreads false reports or \nmakes false statements likely to cause public alarm, shall be punished \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to five years.\n\n82                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \nReceipt \nof \ndocument \nand \npublication \ndetrimental \nto \nparliamentary democracy \n \n124J. (1) \nAny person or any office bearer of any association or any \nresponsible member or agent of any organization who receives any \ndocument or publication detrimental to parliamentary democracy shall \ndeliver the same without delay to a police officer; and any person, \noffice bearer, member or agent who fails to do so, or who, unless \nauthorized so to do by a police officer not below the rank of \nSuperintendent of Police, communicates to any other person, or \npublishes or causes to be published the contents of any such document \nor publication, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which \nmay extend to ten years. \n \n(2) The document and publication referred to in subsection (1) shall \nbe presumed to be a document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy until the contrary is proved; and where in \nany prosecution under this section it is proved that a person was \ncarrying or had in his possession or under his control a document or \npublication detrimental to parliamentary democracy he shall be \ndeemed to have known the contents and the nature of the contents of \nsuch document or publication: \n \nProvided that no person shall be convicted of an offence under this \nsection if he proves to the satisfaction of the court \u2014 \n \n(a) that he was not aware of the contents and the nature of the \ncontents of the document or publication detrimental to \nparliamentary democracy which he was carrying or had in \nhis possession or under his control; and \n \n(b) that he was carrying or had the document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy in his possession \nor under his control in such circumstances that at no time \ndid he have reasonable cause to believe or suspect that the \ndocument or publication was a document or publication \ndetrimental to parliamentary democracy.\n\nPenal Code                                            83 \n \n \nSabotage \n \n124K. Whoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, commits \nsabotage shall be punished with imprisonment for life. \n \n \nAttempt to commit sabotage \n \n124L. Whoever attempts to commit sabotage or does any act \npreparatory thereto shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to fifteen years. \n \n \nEspionage \n \n124M. Whoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, commits \nespionage shall be punished with imprisonment for life. \n \n \nAttempt to commit espionage \n \n124N. Whoever attempts to commit espionage or does any act \npreparatory thereto shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to fifteen years. \n \n \nWaging war against any power in alliance with the Yang  \ndi-Pertuan Agong \n \n125. Whoever whether in conjunction with the enemies of the Yang \ndi-Pertuan Agong or otherwise wages war against the Government of \nany power in alliance or at peace with the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, or \nattempts to wage such war, or abets the waging of such war, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for life, to which fine may be added; or \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to twenty years, to \nwhich fine may be added, or with fine.\n\n84                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nHarbouring or attempting to harbour any person in Malaysia or \nperson residing in a foreign State at war or in hostility against the \nYang di-Pertuan Agong \n \n125A. Whoever by any act, harbours or attempts to harbour, either in \nMalaysia or in the territories of any power at war with, or otherwise in \nactual hostility against, the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, or elsewhere, the \nenemies of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for life, to which fine may be added; or with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to twenty years, to which \nfine may be added, or with fine. \n \n \nCommitting depredation on the territories of any power at peace \nwith the Yang di-Pertuan Agong \n \n126. Whoever whether in conjunction with the enemies of the Yang \ndi-Pertuan Agong or otherwise commits depredation, or makes \npreparations to commit depredation, on the territories of any power in \nalliance or at peace with the Yang di-Pertuan Agong, shall be punished \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to seven years, and \nshall also be liable to fine and to forfeiture of any property used, or \nintended to be used, in committing such depredation, or acquired by \nsuch depredation. \n \n \nReceiving property taken by war or depredation mentioned in \nsections 125 and 126 \n \n127. Whoever receives or attempting to receive any property \nknowing the same to have been taken in the commission of any of the \noffences mentioned in sections 125 and 126, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to seven years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine and to forfeiture of the property so received.\n\nPenal Code                                            85 \n \nPublic servant voluntarily allowing prisoner of State or war in his \ncustody to escape \n \n128. Whoever, being a public servant, and having the custody of any \nprisoner of State or prisoner of war, voluntarily allows such prisoner \nto escape from any place in which such prisoner is confined, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for life, or imprisonment for a term which \nmay extend to twenty years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nPublic servant negligently suffering prisoner of State or war in his \ncustody to escape \n \n129. Whoever, being a public servant, and having the custody of any \nprisoner of State or prisoner of war, negligently suffers such prisoner \nto escape from any place of confinement in which such prisoner is \nconfined, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to three years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nAiding escape of, rescuing, or harbouring such prisoner \n \n130. Whoever knowingly aids or assists any prisoner of State or \nprisoner of war in escaping from lawful custody, or rescues or attempts \nto rescue any such prisoner, or harbours or conceals any such prisoner \nwho has escaped from lawful custody, or offers or attempts to offer \nany resistance to the recapture of such prisoner, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for life, or with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to twenty years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \nExplanation\u2014A prisoner of State or prisoner of war who is permitted to be at \nlarge on his parole within certain limits in Malaysia, is said to escape from lawful \ncustody if he goes beyond the limits within which he is allowed to be at large. \n \n \nInterpretation of this Chapter \n \n130A. \nIn this Chapter\u2014\n\n86                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n(a) \u201cactivity detrimental to parliamentary democracy\u201d means \nan activity carried out by a person or a group of persons \ndesigned to overthrow or undermine parliamentary \ndemocracy by violent or unconstitutional means; \n \n(b) \u201cdocument or publication detrimental to parliamentary \ndemocracy\u201d means any document or publication having in \npart or in whole a tendency \u2014 \n \n(a) to excite organized violence against persons or \nproperty in Malaysia; \n \n(b) to support, propagate or advocate any act \nprejudicial to the security of Malaysia or the \nmaintenance or restoration of public order therein \nor inciting to violence therein or counselling \nviolent disobedience to the law thereof or to any \nlawful order therein; or \n \n(c) to invite, request or demand support for or on \naccount \nof \nany \ncollection, \nsubscription, \ncontribution or donation, whether in money or in \nkind, for the direct or indirect benefit or use of \npersons who intend to act or are about to act, or \nhave acted, in a manner prejudicial to the security \nof Malaysia or to the maintenance of public order \ntherein, or who incite to violence therein or counsel \nviolent disobedience to the law thereof or any \nlawful order therein; \n \n(c) \u201cespionage\u201d means an activity to obtain sensitive \ninformation by ulterior or illegal means for the purpose \nthat is prejudicial to the security or interest of Malaysia; \n \n(d) \u201cessential services\u201d includes\u2014 \n \n(a)  water services; \n \n(b) electricity services;\n\nPenal Code                                            87 \n \n \n(c) public health services; \n \n(d)  banking and financial services; \n \n(e)  fire services; \n \n(f)  prison services;  \n \n(g)  postal services; \n \n(h)  telecommunication \nservices \nincluding \nthe \ncommunication infrastructure; \n \n(i)  telegraph services; \n \n(j)  radio \ncommunication \nservices \nincluding \nbroadcasting and television services; \n \n(k)  port, dock and harbour services and undertakings; \n \n(l)  public transport services by land, sea or air; or \n \n(m)  bulk distribution of fuel and lubricants; \n \n(e) \u201charbour\u201d includes supplying a person with shelter, food, \ndrink, money or clothes; or, except by a person employed \nin a Government hospital, medicines, bandages, surgical \ndressings or any other form of aid to a person wounded; or \narms, ammunition or means of conveyance, or assisting a \nperson in any way to evade apprehension; \n \n(f) \u201cimprisonment for life\u201d means (subject to the provisions \nof any written law conferring power to grant pardons, \nreprieves or respites or suspension or remission of \npunishments) imprisonment until the death of the person \non whom the sentence is imposed; \n \n(g) \u201cpublication\u201d includes all written, pictorial or printed \nmatter, and everything of a nature similar to written or\n\n88                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nprinted matter, whether or not containing any visible \nrepresentation, or by its form, shape or in any other manner \ncapable of suggesting words or ideas, or an audio \nrecording and every copy, translation and reproduction or \nsubstantial translation or reproduction in part or in whole \nthereof; \n \n(h) \u201csabotage\u201d means\u2014 \n \n(a)  an act or omission intending to cause harm\u2014 \n \n (i) for the interests of foreign powers or \nforeign organizations; \n \n(ii) to premises or utilities used for national \ndefence or for war; or \n \n(iii)  to the maintenance of essential services; or \n \n(b) knowingly \nproducing \ndefective \nmaterials, \npremises or utilities used for national defence or \nfor war; \n \n(i) \u201csensitive information\u201d means any document, information \nand material\u2014 \n \n(a) relating to the Cabinet, Cabinet committees and \nState Executive Council; or \n \n(b) that concerns sovereignty, national security, \ndefence, public order and international relations,  \n \nwhether or not classified as \u201cTop Secret\u201d, \u201cSecret\u201d, \n\u201cConfidential\u201d or \u201cRestricted\u201d by a minister, the Menteri \nBesar or Chief Minister of a State or any public officer \nappointed by a minister, the Menteri Besar or Chief \nMinister of a State.\n\nPenal Code                                            89 \n \nCHAPTER VIA \n \nOFFENCES RELATING TO TERRORISM \n \nInterpretation in relation to this Chapter \n \n130B. (1) \nIn this Chapter\u2014 \n \n\u201centity\u201d means a person, group, trust, partnership or fund; \n \n\u201cexplosive or other lethal device\u201d means\u2014 \n \n(a) an explosive or incendiary weapon or device that is \ndesigned or has the capability to cause death, serious \nbodily injury or substantial material damage; or \n \n(b) a weapon or device that is designed or has the capability \nto cause death, serious bodily injury or substantial material \ndamage through the release, dissemination or impact of \ntoxic chemicals, biological agents or toxins or similar \nsubstances or radiation or radioactive material; \n \n\u201charbour\u201d includes supplying a person with shelter, food, drink, \nmoney or clothes; or, except by a person employed in a Government \nhospital, medicine, bandages, surgical dressings or any other form of \naid to a person wounded; or arms, ammunition or means of \nconveyance, or assisting a person in any way to evade apprehension; \n \n\u201cimprisonment for life\u201d means (subject to the provisions of any \nwritten law conferring power to grant pardons, reprieves or respites or \nsuspension or remission of punishments) imprisonment until the death \nof the person on whom the sentence is imposed; \n \n\u201cmaster\u201d, in relation to a vessel, means the owner or person (except \na harbour master or pilot) having for the time being command or charge \nof the vessel; \n \n\u201coperator\u201d, in relation to an aircraft, means the owner or person for \nthe time being in charge or command or control of the aircraft; \n \n\u201cproperty\u201d means\u2014\n\n90                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n(a) assets of every kind, whether corporeal or incorporeal, \nmovable or immovable, tangible or intangible, however \nacquired; or \n \n(b) legal documents or instruments in any form, including \nelectronic or digital, evidencing title to, or interest in, such \nassets, including bank credits, traveller\u2019s cheques, bank \ncheques, money orders, shares, securities, bonds, drafts \nand letters of credit; \n \n\u201cterrorism financing offence\u201d means any offence under section \n130N, 130O, 130P or 130Q; \n \n\u201cterrorist\u201d means any person who\u2014 \n \n(a) commits, or attempts to commit, any terrorist act; or \n \n(b) participates in or facilitates the commission of any terrorist \nact, \n \nand includes a specified entity under section 66B or 66C of the  \n*Anti-Money Laundering, Anti-Terrorism Financing and Proceeds of \nUnlawful Activities Act 2001 [Act 613]; \n \n\u201cterrorist entity\u201d means any entity owned or controlled by any \nterrorist or terrorist group and includes an association of such entities; \n \n\u201cterrorist group\u201d means\u2014 \n \n(a) an entity that has as one of its activities and purposes the \ncommitting of, or the facilitation of the commission of, a \nterrorist act; or \n \n(b) a specified entity under section 66B or 66C of the  \n*Anti-Money Laundering, Anti-Terrorism Financing and \nProceeds of Unlawful Activities Act 2001; \n\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be \n*NOTE\u2014Previously known as the Anti-Money Laundering and Anti-Terrorism Financing Act 2001. \nChange in short title vide section 2 of the Anti-Money Laundering and Anti-Terrorism Financing \n(Amendment) Act 2014 [Act A1467] w.e.f. 1 September 2014\u2014see P.U. (B) 400/2014.\n\nPenal Code                                            91 \n \n \n\u201cterrorist property\u201d means\u2014 \n \n(a) proceeds from the commission of a terrorist act; \n \n(b) property that has been, is being, or is likely to be used to \ncommit a terrorist act; \n \n(c) property that has been, is being, or is likely to be used by \na terrorist, terrorist entity or terrorist group; \n \n(d) property owned or controlled by or on behalf of a terrorist, \nterrorist entity or terrorist group, including funds derived \nor generated from such property; or \n \n(e) property that has been collected for the purpose of \nproviding support to a terrorist, terrorist entity or terrorist \ngroup or funding a terrorist act. \n \n(2) For the purposes of this Chapter, \u201cterrorist act\u201d means an act or \nthreat of action within or beyond Malaysia where\u2014 \n \n(a) the act or threat falls within subsection (3) and does not \nfall within subsection (4); \n \n(b) the act is done or the threat is made with the intention of \nadvancing a political, religious or ideological cause; and \n \n(c) the act or threat is intended or may reasonably be regarded \nas being intended to\u2014 \n \n(i) intimidate the public or a section of the public; or \n \n(ii) influence or compel the Government of Malaysia \nor the Government of any State in Malaysia, any \nother \ngovernment, \nor \nany \ninternational \norganization to do or refrain from doing any act. \n \n(3) An act or threat of action falls within this subsection if it\u2014\n\n92                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n(a) involves serious bodily injury to a person; \n \n(b) endangers a person\u2019s life; \n \n(c) causes a person\u2019s death; \n \n(d) creates a serious risk to the health or the safety of the \npublic or a section of the public; \n \n(e) involves serious damage to property; \n \n(f) involves the use of firearms, explosives or other lethal \ndevices; \n \n(g) involves releasing into the environment or any part of the \nenvironment or distributing or exposing the public or a \nsection of the public to\u2014 \n \n(i) any dangerous, hazardous, radioactive or harmful \nsubstance; \n \n(ii) any toxic chemical; or \n \n(iii) any microbial or other biological agent or toxin; \n \n(h) is designed or intended to disrupt or seriously interfere \nwith, any computer systems or the provision of any \nservices directly related to communications infrastructure, \nbanking or financial services, utilities, transportation or \nother essential infrastructure; \n \n(i) is designed or intended to disrupt, or seriously interfere \nwith, the provision of essential emergency services such \nas police, civil defence or medical services; \n \n(j) involves prejudice to national security or public safety; \n \n(k) involves any combination of any of the acts specified in \nparagraphs (a) to (j),\n\nPenal Code                                            93 \n \n \nand includes any act or omission constituting an offence under the \nAviation Offences Act 1984 [Act 307]. \n \n(4) An act or threat of action falls within this subsection if it\u2014 \n \n(a) is advocacy, protest, dissent or industrial action; and \n \n(b) is not intended\u2014 \n \n(i) to cause serious bodily injury to a person; \n \n(ii) to endanger the life of a person; \n \n(iii) to cause a person\u2019s death; or \n \n(iv) to create a serious risk to the health or safety of the \npublic or a section of the public. \n \n(5) For the purposes of subsection (2)\u2014 \n \n(a) a reference to any person or property is a reference to any \nperson or property wherever situated, within or outside \nMalaysia; and \n \n(b) a reference to the public includes a reference to the public \nof a country or territory other than Malaysia. \n \n \nSuppression of terrorist acts and support for terrorist acts \n \n \nCommitting terrorist acts \n \n130C. \n(1) Whoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, commits \na terrorist act shall be punished\u2014 \n \n(a) if the act results in death, with death; and \n \n(b) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less\n\n94                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n(2) Where in any criminal proceeding it is necessary to decide \nwhether any item or substance is a weapon, a hazardous, radioactive \nor harmful substance, a toxic chemical or a microbial or other \nbiological agent or toxin, a certificate purporting to be signed by an \nappropriate authority to the effect that the item or substance described \nin the certificate is a weapon, a hazardous, radioactive or harmful \nsubstance, a toxic chemical or a microbial or other biological agent or \ntoxin shall be sufficient evidence of the facts stated in it. \n \n \nProviding devices to terrorist groups \n \n130D. \nWhoever knowingly provides or offers to provide any \nexplosive or other lethal device to\u2014 \n \n(a) a terrorist group; \n \n(b) a member of a terrorist group; or \n \n(c) any other person for use by, or for the benefit of, a terrorist \ngroup or a member of a terrorist group, \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for life or imprisonment for a \nterm not exceeding thirty years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nRecruiting persons to be members of terrorist groups or to \nparticipate in terrorist acts \n \n130E. \nWhoever knowingly recruits, or agrees to recruit, another \nperson to be a member of a terrorist group or to participate in the \ncommission of a terrorist act shall be punished with imprisonment for \na term which may extend to thirty years, and shall also be liable to fine.\n\nPenal Code                                            95 \n \nProviding training and instruction to terrorist groups and persons \ncommitting terrorist acts \n \n130F. \nWhoever knowingly provides training or instruction, or \nagrees to provide training or instruction\u2014 \n \n(a) in the making or use of any explosive or other lethal \ndevice; \n \n(b) in carrying out a terrorist act; or \n \n(c) in the practice of military exercises or movements, \n \nto a member of a terrorist group or a person engaging in, or preparing \nto engage in, the commission of a terrorist act shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n \nReceiving training and instruction from terrorist groups and \npersons committing terrorist acts  \n \n130FA. Whoever receives training or instruction, or agrees or \narranges to receive training or instruction\u2014  \n \n(a) in the making or use of any explosive or other lethal device; \n \n(b) in carrying out a terrorist act; or  \n \n(c) in the practice of military exercises or movements,  \n \nfrom a member of a terrorist group or a person engaging in, or \npreparing to engage in, the commission of a terrorist act shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to thirty \nyears, and shall also be liable to fine.\n\n96                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nAttendance at place used for terrorist training  \n \n130FB. (1) Whoever attends at any place, within or outside \nMalaysia\u2014  \n \n(a) knowing or having reason to believe that instruction or \ntraining is being provided there wholly or partly for the \npurposes connected with the commission or preparation of \na terrorist act; or  \n \n(b) where he could not reasonably have failed to understand \nthat instruction or training was being provided there wholly \nor partly for such purposes,  \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to \nten years, or with fine.  \n \n(2) For the purposes of this section, it shall be irrelevant\u2014  \n \n(a) whether the person concerned receives the instruction or \ntraining himself; and  \n \n(b) whether the instruction or training is provided for purposes \nconnected with one or more particular terrorist act.  \n \n(3) References in this section to instruction or training being \nprovided include references to instruction or training being made \navailable. \n \n \nInciting, promoting or soliciting property for the commission of \nterrorist acts \n \n130G. \nWhoever knowingly\u2014 \n \n(a) incites or promotes the commission of a terrorist act; \n \n(b) incites or promotes membership in a terrorist group; or\n\nPenal Code                                            97 \n \n(c) solicits property for the benefit of a terrorist group or for \nthe commission of a terrorist act, \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to \nthirty years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nProviding facilities in support of terrorist acts \n \n130H. \nWhoever being\u2014 \n \n(a) the owner, occupier, lessee or person in charge of any \nbuilding, premises, room or place knowingly permits a \nmeeting of persons to be held in that building, premises, \nroom or place; \n \n(b) the master, charterer, lessee, operator or agent of a vessel \nor the operator, charterer, lessee, agent or pilot in charge \nof an aircraft knowingly permits that vessel or aircraft to \nbe used; or \n \n(c) the owner, lessee or person in charge of any equipment or \nfacility that allows for recording or conferencing or \nmeetings via technology knowingly permits that \nequipment or facility to be used, \n \nfor the purposes of committing an offence under this Chapter, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to thirty \nyears, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nDirecting activities of terrorist groups \n \n130I. \nWhoever intentionally directs the activities of a terrorist \ngroup shall be punished\u2014 \n \n(a) if the act results in death, with death; and \n \n(b) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall\n\n98                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n \nSoliciting or giving support to terrorist groups or for the \ncommission of terrorist acts \n \n130J. \n(1) Whoever knowingly and in any manner solicits support \nfor, or gives support to\u2014 \n \n(a) any terrorist group; or \n \n(b) the commission of a terrorist act, \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for life or imprisonment for a \nterm not exceeding thirty years, or with fine, and shall also be liable to \nforfeiture of any property used or intended to be used in connection \nwith the commission of the offence. \n \n(2) \nFor the purposes of subsection (1), \u201csupport\u201d includes\u2014 \n \n(a) an offer to provide, or the provision of, forged or falsified \ntravel documents to a member of a terrorist group; \n \n(b) an offer to provide, or the provision of, a skill or an \nexpertise for the benefit of, at the direction of or in \nassociation with a terrorist group; \n \n(c) entering or remaining in any country for the benefit of, or \nat the direction of or in association with a terrorist group; \n \n(d) becoming a member of or professing membership of a \nterrorist group; \n \n(e) arranging, managing or assisting in arranging or managing \na meeting to further the activities of a terrorist group; \n  \n(f) using or possessing property for the purpose of committing \nor facilitating the commission of a terrorist act;\n\nPenal Code                                            99 \n \n(g) accumulating, stockpiling or otherwise keeping firearms, \nexplosives, ammunition, poisons or weapons to further the \nactivities of a terrorist group; \n \n(h) arranging, managing or assisting in arranging or managing \nthe transportation of persons to further the activities of a \nterrorist group; \n \n(i) travelling to, entering or remaining in any foreign country to \nfurther the activities of a terrorist group or to commit a \nterrorist act; \n \n(j) encouraging or inducing any person to leave Malaysia to \nfurther the activities of a terrorist group or to commit a \nterrorist act; or \n \n(k) using social media or any other means to\u2014 \n \n(i) advocate for or to promote a terrorist group, support \nfor a terrorist group or the commission of a terrorist \nact; or \n \n(ii) further or facilitate the activities of a terrorist group. \n \n \nTravelling to, through or from Malaysia for the commission of \nterrorist acts in foreign country  \n \n130JA. Whoever, whether or not a citizen or permanent resident of \nMalaysia, travels to, through or from Malaysia with intent to travel to \na foreign country or any part of that foreign country, whether directly \nor through any other country or territory, for the purpose of the \ncommission or the preparation for the commission of a terrorist act in \na foreign country shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to thirty years, and shall also be liable to fine.\n\n100                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nPossession, etc. of items associated with terrorist groups or \nterrorist acts  \n \n130JB. (1) Whoever\u2014  \n \n(a) has possession, custody or control of; or  \n \n(b) provides, displays, distributes or sells,  \n \nany item associated with any terrorist group or the commission of a \nterrorist act shall be punished with imprisonment for a term not \nexceeding seven years, or with fine, and shall also be liable to forfeiture \nof any such item.  \n \n(2) In this section\u2014  \n \n\u201citem\u201d includes publications, visual recordings, flags, banners, \nemblems, insignia and any other thing displaying symbols associated \nwith a terrorist group, terrorist act or ideology of a terrorist group;  \n \n\u201cpublications\u201d includes all written, pictorial or printed matter, and \neverything of a nature similar to written or printed matter, whether or \nnot containing any visible representation, or by its form, shape or in \nany other manner capable of suggesting words or ideas, or an audio \nrecording and every copy, translation and reproduction or substantial \ntranslation or reproduction in part or in whole thereof.  \n \n \nOffence to build, etc. conveyance for use in terrorist acts  \n \n130JC. Whoever\u2014 \n \n(a) builds or agrees to build or causes to be built any \nconveyance with intent or knowledge or having reasonable \ngrounds to believe that the conveyance will be employed in \nor by a terrorist group to further the activities of a terrorist \ngroup or to commit a terrorist act;  \n \n(b) issues or delivers any commission for any conveyance with\n\nPenal Code                                            101 \n \nintent or knowledge or having reasonable grounds to \nbelieve that the conveyance will be employed in or by a \nterrorist group to further the activities of a terrorist group \nor to commit a terrorist act;  \n \n(c)  equips any conveyance with intent or knowledge or having \nreasonable grounds to believe that the conveyance will be \nemployed in or by a terrorist group to further the activities of \na terrorist group or to commit a terrorist act; or  \n \n(d) dispatches or causes or allows to be dispatched any \nconveyance with intent or knowledge or having reasonable \ngrounds to believe that the conveyance will be employed in \nor by a terrorist group to further the activities of a terrorist \ngroup or to commit a terrorist act,  \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for a term not exceeding thirty \nyears, or with fine, and shall also be liable to forfeiture of any such \nconveyance.  \n \n \nPreparation of terrorist acts  \n \n130JD. (1) Whoever, with the intention of committing a terrorist act \nor assisting another to commit a terrorist act, engages in any conduct \nin preparation for giving effect to such intention shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term not exceeding seven years, and shall also be \nliable to fine.  \n \n(2) For the purposes of subsection (1), it shall be irrelevant whether \nthe intention and preparation relate to one or more particular terrorist \nact. \n \n \nHarbouring persons committing terrorist acts \n \n130K. \nWhoever harbours, or prevents, hinders or interferes with the \narrest of any person knowing or having reason to believe that such \nperson\u2014\n\n102                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n(a) has committed or is planning or is likely to commit a \nterrorist act; or \n \n(b) is a member of a terrorist group, \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for life, and shall also be liable \nto fine; or with imprisonment for a term which may extend to twenty \nyears, or with fine. \n \n \nMember of a terrorist group \n \n130KA. Whoever is a member of a terrorist group shall be punished \nwith imprisonment which may extend to imprisonment for life and \nshall also be liable to a fine. \n \n \nCriminal conspiracy \n \n130L. (1) \nWhoever conspires with another person who is in \nMalaysia to do any act without and beyond Malaysia, being an act, \nwhich if done in Malaysia would have constituted an offence under \nthis Chapter shall be deemed to have criminally conspired to do that \nact in Malaysia. \n \n(2) \nWhoever conspires with another person in any place without \nand beyond Malaysia to do any act in Malaysia that constitutes an \noffence under this Chapter shall be deemed to have criminally \nconspired in Malaysia to do that act. \n \n \nIntentional omission to give information relating to terrorist acts \n \n130M. \nWhoever knowing or having reason to believe that any \noffence punishable under sections 130C to 130L has been or will be \ncommitted intentionally omits to give any information respecting that \noffence, which he is legally bound to give, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to seven years or with fine \nor with both.\n\nPenal Code                                            103 \n \n \n \nSuppression of financing of terrorist acts \n \nProviding or collecting property for terrorist acts \n \n130N. \nWhoever, by any means, directly or indirectly, provides or \ncollects or makes available any property intending, knowing or having \nreasonable grounds to believe that the property will be used, in whole \nor in part, to commit a terrorist act shall be punished\u2014 \n \n(a) if the act results in death, with death; and \n \n(b) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine, \n \nand shall also be liable to forfeiture of any property so provided or \ncollected or made available. \n \n \nProviding services for terrorist purposes \n \n130O. (1) Whoever, directly or indirectly, provides or makes \navailable financial services or facilities\u2014 \n \n(a) intending that the services or facilities be used, or knowing \nor having reasonable grounds to believe that the services \nor facilities will be used, in whole or in part, for the \npurpose of committing or facilitating the commission of a \nterrorist act, or for the purpose of benefiting any person \nwho is committing or facilitating the commission of a \nterrorist act; or \n \n(b) knowing or having reasonable grounds to believe that, in \nwhole or in part, the services or facilities will be used by \nor will benefit any terrorist, terrorist entity or terrorist \ngroup,  \n \nshall be punished\u2014\n\n104                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \n(aa) if the act results in death, with death; and \n \n(bb) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n(2) For the purposes of subsection (1), \u201cfinancial services or \nfacilities\u201d includes the services and facilities offered by lawyers and \naccountants acting as nominees or agents for their clients. \n \n \nArranging for retention or control of terrorist property \n \n130P. \nWhoever knowingly enters into an arrangement that \nfacilitates the acquisition, retention or control by or on behalf of \nanother person of terrorist property by concealment, by a removal out \nof jurisdiction, by transfer to a nominee or in any other way shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to thirty \nyears, and shall also be liable to fine and to forfeiture of any property \nso acquired, retained or controlled. \n \n \nDealing with terrorist property \n \n130Q. \n(1) Whoever knowingly deals, directly or indirectly, in any \nterrorist property shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to twenty years, or with fine and shall also be liable \nto forfeiture of any property so dealt with. \n \n(2) \nFor the purposes of subsection (1), \u201cdeals in\u201d includes\u2014 \n \n(a) acquiring or possessing any terrorist property; \n \n(b) entering into or facilitating, directly or indirectly, any \ntransaction in respect of terrorist property; \n \n(c) converting, concealing or disguising terrorist property; or\n\nPenal Code                                            105 \n \n(d) providing any financial or other services in respect of any \nterrorist property to or for the benefit of, or at the direction \nor order of, any terrorist, terrorist entity or terrorist group. \n \n \nAccepting gratification to facilitate or enable terrorist acts \n \n130QA. Whoever accepts gratification to facilitate or enable the \ncommission of any terrorist act shall be punished\u2014 \n \n(a) if the act results in death, with death; and \n \n(b) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n \nIntentional omission to give information about terrorist property \n \n130R. \nWhoever\u2014 \n \n(a) having possession, custody or control of any terrorist \nproperty; or \n \n(b) having information about any transaction or proposed \ntransaction in respect of any terrorist property, \n \nintentionally omits to give any information respecting that matter, \nwhich he is legally bound to give, shall be punished with imprisonment \nfor a term which may extend to seven years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nIntentional omission to give information relating to terrorism \nfinancing offence \n \n130S. \nWhoever knowing or having reason to believe that any \noffence punishable under section 130N, 130O, 130P or 130Q has been \nor will be committed intentionally omits to give any information \nrespecting that offence, which he is legally bound to give, shall be\n\n106                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to seven \nyears or with fine or with both. \n \n \nOffences by body corporate \n \n130T. \nWhere an offence under section 130N, 130O, 130P  or 130Q \nhas been committed by a body corporate, any person who, at the time \nof the commission of the offence, was a person responsible for the \nmanagement or control of the body corporate, which includes a \ndirector, manager, secretary or other similar officer of the body \ncorporate or a person who was purporting to act in any such capacity, \nshall be guilty of that offence and shall be liable to be proceeded \nagainst and punished accordingly unless he proves that\u2014 \n \n(a) the offence was committed without his consent or \nconnivance; and \n \n(b) he had exercised all such due diligence to prevent the \ncommission of the offence as he ought to have exercised, \nhaving regard to the nature of his functions in that capacity \nand to all the circumstances. \n \n \nNon-application of Offenders Compulsory Attendance Act 1954 \nand sections 173A, 293 and 294 of the Criminal Procedure Code  \n \n130TA. The Offenders Compulsory Attendance Act 1954 [Act 461] \nand sections 173A, 293 and 294 of the Criminal Procedure Code shall \nnot apply to an offence under this Chapter. \n \n \nCHAPTER VIB \n \nORGANIZED CRIME \n \nInterpretation in relation to this Chapter \n \n130U. \nIn this Chapter \u2014\n\nPenal Code                                            107 \n \n \n\u201corganized criminal group\u201d means a group of two or more persons, \nacting in concert with the aim of committing one or more serious \noffences, in order to obtain, directly or indirectly, a material benefit, \npower or influence. \n \n \nMember of an organized criminal group \n \n130V. (1) \nWhoever is a member of an organized criminal group \nshall be punished with imprisonment for a term *of not less than five \nyears and not more than twenty years. \n \n(2) Until the contrary is proved, a person shall be presumed to be a \nmember of an organized criminal group where\u2014 \n \n(a) such person can be identified as belonging to an organized \ncriminal group; or \n  \n(b) such person is found with a scheduled weapon as specified \nunder the Corrosive and Explosive Substances and \nOffensive Weapons Act 1958 [Act 357]. \n \n \nAssisting an organized criminal group \n \n130W. Whoever assists an organized criminal group to further the \ninterest of that group shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to ten years. \n \n \nHarbouring member of an organized criminal group \n \n130X. Whoever harbours, or prevents, hinders or interferes with the \narrest of a member of an organized criminal group shall be punished \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to five years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be \n*NOTE\u2014Previously \u201cwhich may extend to five years\u201d\u2013see section 7 of Penal Code \n(Amendment) Act 2014 [Act A1471].\n\n108                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \nConsorting with an organized criminal group \n \n130Y. Whoever without reasonable excuse, consorts with a member \nof an organized criminal group shall be punished with imprisonment \nfor a term of not less than five years and not more than twenty years, \nand shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nRecruiting persons to be members of an organized criminal group \n \n130Z. Whoever knowingly recruits, or agrees to recruit, another \nperson to be a member of an organized criminal group shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to ten years, \nand shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nParticipation in an organized criminal group \n \n130ZA. Whoever participates in an organized criminal group\u2014 \n \n(a) knowing or having reason to believe that it is an organized \ncriminal group; and \n \n(b) knowing, or having reason to believe that, or being reckless \nas to whether, his participation in that group contributes to \nthe occurrence of any criminal activity, \n \nshall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to \nten years, and shall be liable to fine. \n \n \nAccepting gratification to facilitate or enable organized criminal \nactivity \n \n130ZB. Whoever accepts gratification to facilitate or enable any \norganized criminal activity shall be punished\u2014 \n \n(a) if the act results in death, with death; and\n\nPenal Code                                            109 \n \n \n(b) in any other case, with imprisonment for a term of not less \nthan seven years but not exceeding thirty years, and shall \nalso be liable to fine. \n \n \nEnhanced penalties for offences committed by an organized \ncriminal group or member of an organized criminal group \n \n130ZC. (1) Any organized criminal group or a member of an \norganized criminal group convicted of any serious offence under this \nCode or under any written law shall be punished with imprisonment \nfor a term of twice as long as the maximum term for which he would \nhave been liable on conviction for that offence, and shall also be liable \nto whipping. \n \n(2) \nAny organized criminal group or a member of an organized \ncriminal group convicted of any non-serious offence under this Code \nor under any written law shall be punished with imprisonment for a \nterm of not less than two years and not more than twice as long as the \nmaximum term for which he would have been liable on conviction for \nthat offence, and shall also be liable to whipping. \n \n \nCHAPTER VII \n \nOFFENCES RELATING TO THE ARMED FORCES \n \nAbetting mutiny, or attempting to seduce a soldier or sailor from \nhis duty \n \n131. Whoever abets the committing of mutiny by an officer, soldier, \nsailor or airman in the Malaysian Armed Forces, or attempts to seduce \nany such officer, soldier, sailor or airman from his allegiance or his \nduty, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to twenty years, and shall also be liable to fine.\n\n110                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nAbetment of mutiny, if mutiny is committed in consequence \nthereof \n \n132. Whoever abets the committing of mutiny by an officer, soldier, \nsailor or airman in the Malaysian Armed Forces, shall, if mutiny is \ncommitted in consequence of that abetment, be punished with death or \nwith imprisonment for a term which may extend to twenty years, and \nshall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nAbetment of an assault by a soldier or sailor on his superior officer, \nwhen in the execution of his office \n \n133. Whoever abets an assault by an officer, soldier, sailor or airman \nin the Malaysian Armed Forces on any superior officer being in the \nexecution of his office, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to three years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nAbetment of such assault if the assault is committed \n \n134. Whoever abets an assault by an officer, soldier, sailor or airman \nin the Malaysian Armed Forces on any superior officer being in the \nexecution of his office, shall, if such assault is committed in \nconsequence of that abetment, be punished with imprisonment for a \nterm which may extend to seven years, and shall also be liable to fine. \n \n \nAbetment of the desertion of a soldier, sailor or airman \n \n135. Whoever abets the desertion of any officer, soldier, sailor or \nairman in the Malaysian Armed Forces shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to two years or with fine \nor with both. \n \n \nHarbouring a deserter \n \n136. Whoever, except as hereinafter excepted, knowing or having\n\nPenal Code                                            111 \n \nreason to believe that an officer, soldier, sailor or airman in the \nMalaysian Armed Forces has deserted, harbours such officer, soldier, \nsailor or airman, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which \nmay extend to two years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nException\u2014This provision does not extend to the case in which the harbour \nis given by a wife to her husband. \n \n \nDeserter concealed on board merchant vessel through negligence \nof master \n \n137. The master or person in charge of a merchant vessel, on board \nof which any deserter from the Malaysian Armed Forces is concealed, \nshall, though ignorant of such concealment, be liable to a penalty not \nexceeding one thousand ringgit, if he might have known of such \nconcealment, but for some neglect of his duty as such master or person \nin charge, or but for some want of discipline on board of the vessel. \n \n \nAbetment of act of insubordination by a soldier, sailor or airman \n \n138. Whoever abets what he knows to be an act of insubordination \nby an officer, soldier, sailor or airman in the Malaysian Armed Forces \nshall, if such act of insubordination is committed in consequence of \nthat abetment, be punished with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to six months or with fine or with both. \n \n \nPersons subject to Articles of War not punishable under this Code \n \n139. Where provision is made in any written law relating to the \ndiscipline of any of the Malaysian Armed Forces for the punishment of \nan offence corresponding to an offence defined in this Chapter, no person \nwho is subject to such provision shall be subject to punishment under this \nCode for the offence defined in this Chapter.\n\n112                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nWearing the dress of a soldier, sailor or airman \n \n140. Whoever, not being a soldier, sailor or airman in the military, \nnaval or air service of the Yang di-Pertuan Agong wears any garb, or \ncarries any token resembling any garb or token used by such a soldier, \nsailor or airman with the intention that it may be believed that he is \nsuch a soldier, sailor or airman shall be punished with imprisonment \nfor a term which may extend to three months, or with fine which may \nextend to one thousand ringgit or with both. \n \n \n\u201cHarbour\u201d \n \n140A. In this Chapter the word \u201charbour\u201d includes the supplying a \nperson with shelter, food, drink, money, clothes, arms, ammunition, or \nmeans of conveyance, or assisting a person in any way to evade \napprehension. \n \n \nApplication of Chapter VII \n \n140B. \nThe provisions of this Chapter relating to offences committed \nin relation to officers or soldiers in the Malaysian Armed Forces shall \napply mutatis mutandis to similar acts committed in relation to\u2014 \n \n(a)\u2013(c) (Deleted by L.N. (N.S.) 1 of 1957); \n \n(d) \nmembers of the police forces of Malaysia or of the \nRepublic of Singapore; \n \n(e)\u2013(f) \n(Deleted by L.N. (N.S.) 1 of 1957).\n\nPenal Code                                            113 \n \nCHAPTER VIII \n \nOFFENCES AGAINST THE PUBLIC TRANQUILITY \n \nUnlawful assembly \n \n141. An assembly of five or more persons is designated an \u201cunlawful \nassembly\u201d, if the common object of the persons composing that \nassembly is\u2014 \n \n(a) to overawe by criminal force, or show of criminal force, \nthe Legislative or Executive Government of Malaysia or \nany State, or any public servant in the exercise of the \nlawful power of such public servant; \n \n(b) to resist the execution of any law, or of any legal process; \n \n(c) to commit any mischief or criminal trespass, or other \noffence; \n \n(d) by means of criminal force, or show of criminal force, to \nany person, to take or obtain possession of any property, \nor to deprive any person of the enjoyment of a right of \nway, or of use of water or other incorporeal right of which \nhe is in possession or enjoyment, or to enforce any right or \nsupposed right; or \n \n(e) by means of criminal force, or show of criminal force, to \ncompel any person to do what he is not legally bound to \ndo, or to omit to do what he is legally entitled to do. \n \nExplanation\u2014An assembly which was not unlawful when it assembled may \nsubsequently become an unlawful assembly. \n \n \nBeing a member of an unlawful assembly \n \n142. Whoever, being aware of facts which render any assembly an \nunlawful assembly, intentionally joins that assembly, or continues in \nit, is said to be a member of an unlawful assembly.\n\n114                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \nPunishment \n \n143. Whoever is a member of an unlawful assembly, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to six \nmonths or with fine or with both. \n \n \nPossessing weapons or missiles at unlawful assemblies \n \n144. Any person who attends, takes part in or is found at any \nunlawful assembly and who has in his possession at such assembly any \nfirearm, ammunition, explosive, corrosive, injurious or obnoxious \nsubstance, stick, stone or any weapon or missile capable of use as a \nweapon of offence shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to two years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nJoining or continuing in an unlawful assembly, knowing that it has \nbeen commanded to disperse \n \n145. Whoever joins or continues in an unlawful assembly, knowing \nthat such unlawful assembly has been commanded in the manner \nprescribed by law to disperse, shall be punished with imprisonment for \na term which may extend to two years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nForce used by one member in prosecution of common object \n \n146. Whenever force or violence is used by an unlawful assembly or \nby any member thereof, in prosecution of the common object of such \nassembly, every member of such assembly is guilty of the offence of \nrioting. \n \n \nPunishment for rioting \n \n147. Whoever is guilty of rioting shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to two years or with fine\n\nPenal Code                                            115 \n \nor with both. \n \n \nPossessing weapons or missiles at riot \n \n148. Any person who attends, takes part in or is found at any riot and \nwho has in his possession at such riot any firearm, ammunition, \nexplosive, corrosive, injurious or obnoxious substance, stick, stone or \nany weapon or missile capable of use as a weapon of offence shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to five years \nor with fine or with both. \n \n \nEvery member of an unlawful assembly to be deemed guilty of any \noffence committed in prosecution of common object \n \n149. If an offence is committed by any member of an unlawful \nassembly in prosecution of the common object of that assembly, or \nsuch as the members of that assembly knew to be likely to be \ncommitted in prosecution of that object, every person who, at the time \nof the committing of that offence, is a member of the same assembly, \nis guilty of that offence. \n \n \nHiring, or conniving at hiring, of persons to join an unlawful \nassembly \n \n150. Whoever hires or engages or employs, or promotes or connives \nat the hiring, engagement, or employment of any person to join or \nbecome a member of any unlawful assembly shall be punishable as a \nmember of such  unlawful assembly, and for any offence which may \nbe committed by any such person as a member of such unlawful \nassembly, in pursuance of such hiring, engagement, or employment, in \nthe same manner as if he had been a  member of such unlawful \nassembly, or himself had committed such offence.\n\n116                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nKnowingly joining or continuing in any assembly of five or more \npersons after it has been commanded to disperse \n \n151. Whoever knowingly joins or continues in any assembly of five \nor more persons likely to cause a disturbance of the public peace, after \nsuch assembly has been lawfully commanded to disperse, shall be \npunished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to six \nmonths or with fine or with both. \n \n \nExplanation\u2014If the assembly is an unlawful assembly within the meaning \nof section 141, the offender will be punishable under section 145. \n \n \nAssaulting or obstructing public servant when suppressing riot, \netc. \n \n152. Whoever assaults or threatens to assault, or obstructs or attempts \nto obstruct, to any public servant in the discharge of his duty as such \npublic servant in endeavouring to disperse an unlawful assembly or to \nsuppress a riot or affray, or uses, or threatens or attempts to use, \ncriminal force to such public servant, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to three years or with fine \nor with both. \n \n \nWantonly giving provocation, with intent to cause riot \n \n153. Whoever malignantly or wantonly, by doing anything which is \nillegal, gives provocation to any person, intending or knowing it to be \nlikely that such provocation will cause the offence of rioting to be \ncommitted, shall, if the offence of rioting is committed in consequence \nof such provocation, be punished with imprisonment for a term which \nmay extend to  one year, or with fine, or with both; and if the offence \nof rioting is not committed, with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to six months or with fine or with both. \n \n \n153A. \n(Deleted by F.M.S. En. 13 of 1939).\n\nPenal Code                                            117 \n \n \nOwner or occupier of land on which an unlawful assembly is held \n \n154. Whenever any unlawful assembly or riot takes place, the owner \nor occupier of the land upon which such unlawful assembly is held or \nsuch riot is committed, and any person having or claiming an interest \nin such land, shall be punishable with fine not exceeding two thousand \nringgit, if he or his agent or manager, knowing that such offence is \nbeing or has been committed, or having reason to believe it is likely to \nbe committed, do not give the earliest notice thereof, in his or their \npower to the principal officer at the  nearest police station, and do not, \nin the case of his or their having reason to believe that it is about to be \ncommitted, use all lawful means in his or their power to prevent it, and \nin the event of its taking place, do not use all lawful means in his or \ntheir power to disperse or suppress the riot of unlawful assembly. \n \n \nLiability of person for whose benefit a riot is committed \n \n155. Whenever a riot is committed for the benefit or on behalf of any \nperson who is the owner or occupier of any land respecting which such \nriot takes place, or who claims any interest in such land, or in the \nsubject of any dispute which gave rise to the riot, or who has accepted \nor derived any benefit therefrom, such person shall be punishable with \nfine, if he or his agent or manager, having reason to believe that such \nriot was likely to be committed, or that the unlawful assembly by which \nsuch riot was committed was likely to be held, shall not respectively \nuse all lawful means in his or their power to prevent such assembly or \nriot from taking place, and for suppressing and dispersing the same. \n \n \nLiability of agent of owner or occupier for whose benefit a riot is \ncommitted \n \n156. Whenever a riot is committed for the benefit or on behalf of any \nperson who is the owner or occupier of any land respecting which such \nriot takes place, or who claims any interest in such land, or in the \nsubject of any dispute which gave rise to the riot, or who has accepted \nor derived any benefit therefrom, the agent or manager of such person \nshall be punishable with fine, if such agent or manager, having reason\n\n118                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \nto believe that such riot  was likely to be committed, or that the \nunlawful assembly by which such riot was committed was likely to be \nheld, shall not use all lawful means in his power to prevent such riot or \nassembly from taking place, and for suppressing and dispersing the \nsame. \n \n \nHarbouring persons hired for an unlawful assembly \n \n157. Whoever harbours, receives, or assembles in any house or \npremises in his occupation or charge, or under his control, any persons, \nknowing that such persons have been hired, engaged, or employed, or \nare about to be hired, engaged, or employed, to join or become \nmembers of an unlawful assembly, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to six months or with fine \nor with both. \n \n \nBeing hired to take part in an unlawful assembly or riot, or to go \narmed \n \n158. Whoever is engaged or hired, or offers or attempts to be hired \nor engaged, to do or assist in doing any of the acts specified in  \nsection 141, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which \nmay extend to six months or with fine or with both; and whoever, being \nso engaged or hired as aforesaid, goes armed, or engages or offers to \ngo armed, with any deadly weapon, or with anything which used as a \nweapon of offence is likely to cause death, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term  which may extend to two years or  with fine \nor with both. \n \n \n*ILLUSTRATION \n \nThe last section is subject to the same illustration as section 144. \n \n \n\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be\uf0be \n*NOTE\u2014 Illustration to section 144 was deleted by Act 39 of 1967. It read as follows \u201cA wooden pole \nsharpened at the end is a thing which, used as a weapon of offence, is likely to cause death\u201d.\n\nPenal Code                                            119 \n \nAffray \n \n159. When two or more persons, by fighting, in a public place, \ndisturb the public peace, they are said to \u201ccommit an affray\u201d. \n \n \nPunishment for committing affray \n \n160. Whoever commits an affray shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to six months, or with fine \nwhich may extend to one thousand ringgit or with both. \n \n \nCHAPTER IX \n \nOFFENCES BY, OR RELATING TO, PUBLIC SERVANTS \n \n \nPublic servant taking a gratification, other than legal \nremuneration, in respect of an official act \n \n161. Whoever, being or expecting to be a public servant, accepts or \nobtains, or agrees to accept or attempts to obtain, from any person, for \nhimself or for any other person, any gratification whatever, other than \nlegal remuneration, as a motive or reward for doing or forbearing to do \nany official act, or for showing or forbearing to show, in the exercise \nof his official functions, favour or disfavour to any person, or for \nrendering or attempting to render any service or disservice to any \nperson, with the Government, or with any member of the Cabinet or of \nParliament or of a State Executive Council or Legislative Assembly, \nor with any public servant, as such, shall be punished with \nimprisonment for a term which may extend to three years or with fine \nor with both. \n \n \nExplanations\u2014\u201cExpecting to be a public servant\u201d. If a person not expecting \nto be in office obtains a gratification by deceiving others into a belief that he is \nabout to be in office, and that he will then serve them, he may be guilty of \ncheating, but he is not guilty of the offence defined in this section. \n \n\u201cGratification\u201d. The word \u201cgratification\u201d is not restricted to pecuniary \ngratifications, or to gratifications estimable in money.\n\n120                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \n\u201cLegal remuneration\u201d. The words \u201clegal remuneration\u201d are not restricted to \nremuneration which a public servant can lawfully demand, but include all \nremuneration which he is permitted by law to accept. \n \n \u201cA motive or reward for doing\u201d. A person who receives a gratification as a \nmotive for doing what he does not intend to do, or as a reward for doing what he \nhas not done, comes within these words. \n \n \nILLUSTRATIONS \n \n(a) A, a Judge, obtains from Z, a banker, a situation in Z\u2019s bank for A\u2019s \nbrother, as a reward to A for deciding a cause in favour of Z. A has committed \nthe offence defined in this section. \n \n(b)  A, a public servant, induces Z erroneously to believe that A\u2019s influence \nwith the Chairman of a Town Board has obtained for Z a contract to do work, \nand thus induces Z to give A money. A has committed the offence defined in this \nsection. \n \n(c)  A, a public servant, induces Z erroneously to believe that A\u2019s influence \nwith the Government has obtained a grant of land for Z, and thus induces Z to \ngive A money, as a reward for his service. A has committed the offence defined \nin this section. \n \n \nTaking a gratification in order, by corrupt or illegal means, to \ninfluence a public servant \n \n162. Whoever accepts or obtains, or agrees to accept or attempts to \nobtain, from any person, for himself or for any other person, any \ngratification whatever, as a motive or reward for inducing, by corrupt \nor illegal means, any public servant to do or to forbear to do any official \nact, or in the exercise of the official functions of such public servant to \nshow favour or disfavour to any person, or to render or attempt to \nrender any service or disservice to any person with the Government, or \nwith any member of the Cabinet or of Parliament or of a State \nExecutive Council or Legislative Assembly, or with any public \nservant, as such, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term  which \nmay extend to three years or with fine or with both.\n\nPenal Code                                            121 \n \nTaking a gratification, for the exercise of personal influence with \na public servant \n \n163. Whoever accepts or obtains, or agrees to accept or attempts to \nobtain, from any person, for himself or for any other person, any \ngratification  whatever, as a motive or reward for inducing, by the \nexercise of personal influence, any public servant to do or to forbear to \ndo any official act, or in the exercise of the official functions of such \npublic servant to show favour or disfavour to any person, or to render \nor attempt to render any service or disservice to any person with the \nGovernment, or with any member of the Cabinet or of Parliament or \nof a State Executive Council or Legislative Assembly, or with any \npublic servant, as such, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term \nwhich may extend to one year or with fine or  with both. \n \n \nILLUSTRATION \n \nAn advocate who receives a fee for arguing a case before a Judge; a person \nwho receives pay for arranging and correcting a memorial addressed to \nGovernment, setting forth the services and claims for the memorialist; a paid \nagent for a condemned criminal, who lays before the Government statements \ntending to show that the condemnation was unjust\u2014are not within this section, \ninasmuch as they do not exercise or profess to exercise personal influence. \n \n \nPunishment for abetment by public servant of the offences above \ndefined \n \n164. Whoever, being a public servant, in respect of whom either of \nthe offences defined in sections 162 and 163 is committed, abets the \noffence, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to three years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nILLUSTRATION \n \nA, is a public servant. B, A\u2019s wife, receives a present as a motive for \nsoliciting A to give an office to a particular person. A abets her doing so.  B is \npunishable with imprisonment for a term not exceeding one year or with fine or \nwith both. A is punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to \nthree years or with fine or with both.\n\n122                                         Laws of Malaysia                      ACT 574 \n \n \n \nPublic \nservant \nobtaining \nany \nvaluable \nthing, \nwithout \nconsideration, from person concerned in any proceeding or \nbusiness transacted by such public servant \n \n165. Whoever, being a public servant, accepts or obtains, or agrees \nto accept or attempts to obtain, for himself or for any other person, any \nvaluable thing, without consideration, or for a consideration which he \nknows to be inadequate, from any person whom he knows to have \nbeen, or to be, or to be likely to be concerned in any proceeding or \nbusiness transacted, or about to be transacted, by such public servant, \nor having any connection with the official functions of  himself or of \nany  public servant to whom he is subordinate, or from any person \nwhom he knows to be interested in or related to the person so \nconcerned, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may \nextend to two years or with fine or with both. \n \n \nILLUSTRATIONS \n \n(a) A, a Judge, hires a house of Z, who has a case pending before him. It is \nagreed that A shall pay fifty ringgit a month, the house being such that, if the \nbargain were made in good faith, A would be required to pay two hundred ringgit \na month. A has obtained a valuable thing from Z without adequate consideration. \n \n(b) A, a Judge, buys of Z, who has a cause pending in A\u2019s Court, \nGovernment promissory notes at a discount, when they are selling in the market \nat a premium. A has obtained a valuable thing from Z without adequate \nconsideration. \n \n(c) Z\u2019s brother is apprehended and taken before A, a Magistrate, on a \ncharge of perjury.
